## סְאָה (id: 004979000000000)

סְאָה
=====

סְאָה (H5429)

noun f

Capacity

seah \= unit of dry measure equivalent to 7\.3 liters or 7 quarts; 3 seahs make up 1 ephah

[GEN 18:6](https://ref.ly/Gen18:6) · [1SA 25:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:18) · [1KI 18:32](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:32) · [2KI 7:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:1) · [2KI 7:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:1) · [2KI 7:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:16) · [2KI 7:16](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:16) · [2KI 7:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:18) · [2KI 7:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs7:18)

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 18:6; 1 Samuel 25:18; 1 Kings 18:32; 2 Kings 7:1; 2 Kings 7:16; 2 Kings 7:18


## סְאֹון (id: 004980000000000)

סְאֹון
======

סְאֹון (H5430)

noun m · סאן

Clothing

boot \= covering for the foot and leg ◄ made of leather ► used by soldiers ≈ associated with aggression

[ISA 9:4](https://ref.ly/Isa9:4)

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 9:4


## סאן (id: 004981000000000)

סאן
===

סאן (H5431)

verb · סְאֹון

Move

to tramp \= to walk heavily and firmly; ≈ associated with marching soldiers

[ISA 9:4](https://ref.ly/Isa9:4)

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 9:4


## סַאסְּאָה (id: 004982000000000)

סַאסְּאָה
=========

סַאסְּאָה (H5432) — סאסא

verb

Intense

measure \= state in which a condition has a specific degree of intensity

[ISA 27:8](https://ref.ly/Isa27:8)1

verb

Conflict

quarrel meaning unsure; possibly: \= state of opposition or hostility between two or more persons

[ISA 27:8](https://ref.ly/Isa27:8)1

verb

Angry

fury meaning unsure; possibly: \= state of fierce anger

[ISA 27:8](https://ref.ly/Isa27:8)1

verb

Space

expulsion meaning unsure; possibly: \= causative action by which humans are forced to live their dwelling\-place

[ISA 27:8](https://ref.ly/Isa27:8)1

1 ISA 27:8 RSV ESV "measure" \= \[1a] \| NIV "warfare" REB "quarrel" \= \[2a] \| NJPS "fury" \= \[3a] \| NJB "expelling" NRSV "expulsion" \= \[4a]

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Isaiah 27:8


## סבא (id: 004983000000000)

סבא
===

סבא (H5433a)

verb · סָבָא · סֹבֶא

Ingest

to drink in excess, to be a drunkard \= action by which humans consume alcoholic beverages in large quantities, ► which results in drunkenness and other forms of loose behavior, ≈ and is generally regarded as foolish and unacceptable

[DEU 21:20](https://ref.ly/Deut21:20) · [PRO 23:20](https://ref.ly/Prov23:20) · [PRO 23:21](https://ref.ly/Prov23:21) · [ISA 56:12](https://ref.ly/Isa56:12) · [NAM 1:10](https://ref.ly/Nah1:10)

1 EZK 23:42 MT\-K סובאים \| MT\-Q סָבָאִים \= סָבָא

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 21:20; Proverbs 23:20; Proverbs 23:21; Isaiah 56:12; Nahum 1:10


## סְבָא (id: 004984000000000)

סְבָא
=====

סְבָא (H5434)

name · סְבָאִי

Names of People

Seba \= man; ◄ son of Cush; descendant of Ham ► founder of a nation bearing the same name

[GEN 10:7](https://ref.ly/Gen10:7) · [1CH 1:9](https://ref.ly/1Chr1:9)

Names of Groups

Seba \= ethnic group ◄ founded by Seba, son of Cush, regarded as a descendant of Ham

[PSA 72:10](https://ref.ly/Ps72:10) · [ISA 43:3](https://ref.ly/Isa43:3)

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 10:7; 1 Chronicles 1:9; Psalms 72:10; Isaiah 43:3

סָבָא

סָבָא (H5433b)

Ingest

drunkard \= a person who has the habit of consuming alcoholic beverages in large quantities ► which results in drunkenness and other forms of loose behavior; ≈ regarded as foolish and unacceptable

## סבב (id: 004988000000000)

סבב
===

סבב (H5437 · H4142)

verb · מוּסָב · מֵסַב · נְסִבָּה · סִבָּה · סָבִיב · מְסִבָּה

Turn

to turn, to swing \= process by which a door is attached to a wall by means of a hinge, or a contraption with a similar function, which allows it to pivot

[PRO 26:14](https://ref.ly/Prov26:14) · [EZK 26:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek26:2) · [EZK 41:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek41:24)

Turn

to turn, to turn around \= action by which humans, supernatural beings, forces of nature, or other objects face a direction different from the one they were facing before

[GEN 42:24](https://ref.ly/Gen42:24) · [JDG 18:23](https://ref.ly/Judg18:23) · [1SA 15:27](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:27) · [1SA 17:30](https://ref.ly/1Sam17:30) · [1SA 22:17](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:17) · [1SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:18) · [1SA 22:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:18) · [2SA 18:30](https://ref.ly/2Sam18:30) · [2SA 18:30](https://ref.ly/2Sam18:30) · [1KI 8:14](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:14) · [2KI 9:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:18) · [2KI 9:19](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:19) · [2CH 6:3](https://ref.ly/2Chr6:3) · [2CH 18:31](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:31) · [PSA 114:3](https://ref.ly/Ps114:3) · [PSA 114:5](https://ref.ly/Ps114:5) · [ECC 1:6](https://ref.ly/Eccl1:6) · [ECC 1:6](https://ref.ly/Eccl1:6) · [ECC 1:6](https://ref.ly/Eccl1:6) · [SNG 2:17](https://ref.ly/Song2:17) · [JER 41:14](https://ref.ly/Jer41:14) · [EZK 1:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:9) · [EZK 1:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:12) · [EZK 1:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek1:17) · [EZK 10:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:11) · [EZK 10:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:11) · [EZK 10:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek10:16) · [EZK 42:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek42:19)

Bear

**Collocation:** סבב בְּנֶפֶשׁ

to be responsible for literally, possibly, to turn on (someone's) life; hence: \= state in which someone is held responsible for the death of someone else

[1SA 22:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam22:22)1

Change

to change literally: to turn (a situation); hence: \= causative action by which humans cause a certain condition or process to be different

[NUM 32:38](https://ref.ly/Num32:38) · [2SA 14:20](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:20) · [2KI 23:34](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:34) · [2KI 24:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs24:17) · [2CH 36:4](https://ref.ly/2Chr36:4)

Different

to change literally: to turn; hence: \= process by which an object becomes significantly different

[ZEC 14:10](https://ref.ly/Zech14:10)

Non\-Engage

**Collocation:** סבב פָּנִים

to turn (one's) face, to look away, to leave (someone) alone literally: to turn (one's) face (from someone); hence: \= action by which humans or deities refrain from engaging in an activity involving another party

[2CH 35:22](https://ref.ly/2Chr35:22) · [EZK 7:22](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:22)

Move

**Collocation:** סבב מִפָּנִים

to elude, to evade, to dodge literally: to turn away from (someone's) face; hence: \= action by which humans quickly turn and move away from approaching danger

[1SA 18:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam18:11)

Move

to return, to go back literally: to turn; hence: \= action by which humans return to the place from which they came

[1SA 15:12](https://ref.ly/1Sam15:12) · [2SA 14:24](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:24) · [2SA 14:24](https://ref.ly/2Sam14:24) · [1CH 16:43](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:43)

Move

to go around \= action by which humans move in a full or partial circle

[NUM 21:4](https://ref.ly/Num21:4) · [DEU 2:1](https://ref.ly/Deut2:1) · [DEU 2:3](https://ref.ly/Deut2:3) · [JOS 6:3](https://ref.ly/Josh6:3) · [JOS 6:4](https://ref.ly/Josh6:4) · [JOS 6:7](https://ref.ly/Josh6:7) · [JOS 6:14](https://ref.ly/Josh6:14) · [JOS 6:15](https://ref.ly/Josh6:15) · [JOS 6:15](https://ref.ly/Josh6:15) · [JDG 11:18](https://ref.ly/Judg11:18) · [2SA 5:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam5:23) · [1CH 14:14](https://ref.ly/1Chr14:14) · [2CH 33:14](https://ref.ly/2Chr33:14) · [PSA 26:6](https://ref.ly/Ps26:6) · [PSA 48:13](https://ref.ly/Ps48:13) · [PSA 55:11](https://ref.ly/Ps55:11)

Move

to lead around, to cause to go around \= causative action by which humans or deities cause (other) humans to move in a full or partial circle

[EXO 13:18](https://ref.ly/Exod13:18) · [JOS 6:11](https://ref.ly/Josh6:11) · [2CH 13:13](https://ref.ly/2Chr13:13) · [EZK 47:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek47:2)

Move

to go about \= action by which humans move through a certain place, though not always in a straight line but by changing directions occasionally

[1SA 7:16](https://ref.ly/1Sam7:16) · [2KI 3:9](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:9) · [2CH 17:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr17:9) · [2CH 23:2](https://ref.ly/2Chr23:2) · [PSA 59:7](https://ref.ly/Ps59:7) · [PSA 59:15](https://ref.ly/Ps59:15) · [ECC 12:5](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:5) · [SNG 3:2](https://ref.ly/Song3:2) · [SNG 3:3](https://ref.ly/Song3:3) · [SNG 5:7](https://ref.ly/Song5:7) · [ISA 23:16](https://ref.ly/Isa23:16)

Move

to roll literally: to cause to turn; hence: \= causative action by which humans cause a round object to move by turning it over and over on its axis

[ISA 28:27](https://ref.ly/Isa28:27)

Control

to bring over literally: to cause (a nation) to go around to (a king); hence: \= causative action by which humans cause other humans to take on a position of leadership over a nation

[2SA 3:12](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:12)

Engage

**Collocation:** כֹּוס סבב

to come round literally: a cup comes round; hence: \= process by which humans undergo a certain event when their turn has come

[HAB 2:16](https://ref.ly/Hab2:16)

Engage

to turn over, to transfer literally: to cause to go around; hence: \= causative action by which humans cause other humans to engage with a certain opportunity

[1CH 10:14](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:14) · [1CH 12:24](https://ref.ly/1Chr12:24)

Non\-Engage

to pass literally: to go around; hence: \= process by which humans forfeit an opportunity in favor of someone else

[1KI 2:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs2:15)

Non\-Possess

to pass over, to be transferred literally: to go around (from one party to another); hence: \= process by which the right of possession of a certain piece of land moves from one party to another

[NUM 36:7](https://ref.ly/Num36:7) · [NUM 36:9](https://ref.ly/Num36:9) · [JER 6:12](https://ref.ly/Jer6:12)

Space

to wind literally: to go through; hence: \= process by which a river or passageway takes a twisting or spiraling course from one place to another

[GEN 2:11](https://ref.ly/Gen2:11) · [GEN 2:13](https://ref.ly/Gen2:13) · [EZK 41:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek41:7)

Space

to surround literally: to go around; hence: \= state in which objects are located all around a person or animal

[2SA 22:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:6) · [1KI 7:24](https://ref.ly/1Kgs7:24) · [2CH 4:3](https://ref.ly/2Chr4:3) · [JOB 40:22](https://ref.ly/Job40:22) · [PSA 18:6](https://ref.ly/Ps18:6) · [JON 2:4](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:4) · [JON 2:6](https://ref.ly/Jonah2:6)

Space

to surround literally: to go around; hence: \= action by which groups of humans or animals take position all around an individual, a group, or an object

[GEN 19:4](https://ref.ly/Gen19:4) · [GEN 37:7](https://ref.ly/Gen37:7) · [JOS 7:9](https://ref.ly/Josh7:9) · [JDG 16:2](https://ref.ly/Judg16:2) · [JDG 19:22](https://ref.ly/Judg19:22) · [JDG 20:5](https://ref.ly/Judg20:5) · [2SA 18:15](https://ref.ly/2Sam18:15) · [2KI 3:25](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:25) · [2KI 6:15](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:15) · [2KI 8:21](https://ref.ly/2Kgs8:21) · [2CH 21:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr21:9) · [JOB 16:13](https://ref.ly/Job16:13) · [PSA 7:8](https://ref.ly/Ps7:8) · [PSA 17:11](https://ref.ly/Ps17:11) · [PSA 22:13](https://ref.ly/Ps22:13) · [PSA 22:17](https://ref.ly/Ps22:17) · [PSA 109:3](https://ref.ly/Ps109:3) · [PSA 118:10](https://ref.ly/Ps118:10) · [PSA 118:11](https://ref.ly/Ps118:11) · [PSA 118:11](https://ref.ly/Ps118:11) · [PSA 118:12](https://ref.ly/Ps118:12) · [ECC 9:14](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:14)

Space

to surround literally: to cause to surround; hence: \= causative action by which humans cause a construction to be all around an object

[2CH 14:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr14:6)

Arrange

to sit down around the table literally: to surround; hence: \= action by which humans take their place around a table

[1SA 16:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam16:11)

Bear

to surround \> to be a constant witness literally: to surround; hence: \= state in which humans remain constantly associated with and held responsible for past deeds

[HOS 7:2](https://ref.ly/Hos7:2)

Cover

enclosed, mounted literally: to be surrounded; hence: \= state in which the bottom and the sides of an object are tightly fixed in a mold that keeps it in its place

[EXO 28:11](https://ref.ly/Exod28:11) · [EXO 39:6](https://ref.ly/Exod39:6) · [EXO 39:13](https://ref.ly/Exod39:13)

Dimension

to measure in circumference literally: (a measuring cord of a certain length) surrounds (something); hence: \= state in which a round object has a certain measurable circumference

[1KI 7:15](https://ref.ly/1Kgs7:15) · [1KI 7:23](https://ref.ly/1Kgs7:23) · [2CH 4:2](https://ref.ly/2Chr4:2) · [JER 52:21](https://ref.ly/Jer52:21)

Engage

to be surrounded (with something), to happen in full measure literally: (an activity) surrounds (someone); hence: \= process by which humans undergo a certain activity in full measure

[PSA 32:10](https://ref.ly/Ps32:10) · [PSA 49:6](https://ref.ly/Ps49:6) · [PSA 88:18](https://ref.ly/Ps88:18)

Engage

to surround (someone with something), to cause (something) to happen in full measure literally: to surround (someone with an an activity); hence: \= causative process by which humans or deities cause (other) humans to undergo a certain activity in full measure

[1KI 5:17](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:17) · [PSA 32:7](https://ref.ly/Ps32:7) · [HOS 12:1](https://ref.ly/Hos12:1)

Safe

to surround \> to shield, to protect literally: to surround; hence: \= causative action by which humans or deities provide protection to (other) humans

[DEU 32:10](https://ref.ly/Deut32:10) · [JER 31:22](https://ref.ly/Jer31:22)

Non\-Space

to be removed literally: to go around; hence: \= process by which an object is removed from its place and brought somewhere else

[1SA 5:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:8)

Non\-Space

to be removed literally: to cause to go around; hence: \= causative action by which humans cause an object to be removed from its place and brought somewhere else

[1SA 5:8](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:8) · [1SA 5:9](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:9) · [1SA 5:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam5:10) · [2SA 20:12](https://ref.ly/2Sam20:12) · [2KI 16:18](https://ref.ly/2Kgs16:18) · [1CH 13:3](https://ref.ly/1Chr13:3) · [JER 21:4](https://ref.ly/Jer21:4)

Space

to turn \= state in which the boundary of an area changes direction and continues into a different direction

[NUM 34:4](https://ref.ly/Num34:4) · [NUM 34:5](https://ref.ly/Num34:5) · [JOS 15:3](https://ref.ly/Josh15:3) · [JOS 15:10](https://ref.ly/Josh15:10) · [JOS 16:6](https://ref.ly/Josh16:6) · [JOS 18:14](https://ref.ly/Josh18:14) · [JOS 19:14](https://ref.ly/Josh19:14) · [JER 31:39](https://ref.ly/Jer31:39)

Stance

**Collocation:** סבב עֵינִַים

to turn away (one's) eyes literally: to turn (one's) eyes; hence: \= action by which humans look away from something they have been looking at before

[SNG 6:5](https://ref.ly/Song6:5)

Stance

**Collocation:** סבב פָּנִים

to cause to turn around, to roll literally: to turn (one's) face; hence: \= action by which humans turn their face in a certain direction

[1KI 21:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs21:4) · [2KI 20:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs20:2) · [2CH 29:6](https://ref.ly/2Chr29:6) · [ISA 38:2](https://ref.ly/Isa38:2)

Think

to turn, to change (one's) mind literally: to turn; hence: \= action by which deities change their minds about humans

[PSA 71:21](https://ref.ly/Ps71:21)

Think

**Collocation:** סבב לֵב

to turn (one's) heart, to put (one's) mind (on something else) literally: to turn (one's) heart; hence: \= action by which humans decide to focus their thinking on something else

[ECC 2:20](https://ref.ly/Eccl2:20)2 · [ECC 7:25](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:25)3

Think

**Collocation:** סבב לֵב אֲחֹרַנִּית

to turn (someone's) heart back, to win back (someone's allegiance) literally: to turn back (someone's) heart; hence: \= causative action by which deities cause humans to change their way of thinking

[1KI 18:37](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:37)

Willing

**Collocation:** סבב לֵב

to turn (someone's) heart, to change (someone's) disposition literally: to turn (someone's) heart; hence: \= action by which deities cause humans to have a different opinion about other humans

[EZR 6:22](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:22)

1 1SA 22:22 It is possible that סבתי should be read חבתי. 2 ECC 2:20 The word לֵב "heart" is missing in this clause, though it is found in the next. 3 ECC 7:25 MT וְלִבִּי; we are ignoring the copula.

Reinier de Blois

## סִבָּה (id: 004989000000000)

סִבָּה
======

## סבל (id: 004995000000000)

סבל
===

סבל (H5445 · A5446)

verb · סֵבֶל · סַבָּל · סֹבֶל · סְבָלֹות

Hold

to carry, to bear \= state in which humans endure or sustain the weight of a physical burden

[GEN 49:15](https://ref.ly/Gen49:15) · [ISA 46:7](https://ref.ly/Isa46:7)

Bear

to bear literally: to carry; hence: \= state in which humans endure pains or hardships as a form of punishment

[ISA 53:4](https://ref.ly/Isa53:4) · [ISA 53:11](https://ref.ly/Isa53:11) · [LAM 5:7](https://ref.ly/Lam5:7)

Safe

to carry, to support, to uphold literally: to carry; hence: \= action by which deities provide help and support to the aged and the weak

[ISA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Isa46:4) · [ISA 46:4](https://ref.ly/Isa46:4)

Move

to drag oneself along literally: to carry; hence: \= process by which humans walk with difficulty, ◄ as if they are bearing a heavy load

[ECC 12:5](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:5)

Pregnant

to be with young literally: to carry; hence: \= state in which an animal is pregnant

[PSA 144:14](https://ref.ly/Ps144:14)1

Space

to place, to put in place, to lay exact meaning unknown; possibly: \= causative action by which humans put an object in a certain location

[EZR 6:3](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:3)2

1 PSA 144:14 RSV NRSV ESV "be heavy with young" GNT "reproduce plentifully" CEV "have calves" \| NIV "draw heavy loads" \| NJB "well fed" REB "fat" \| 2 EZR 6:3 NIV "be laid" NJB ESV "be retained" \| LXX "θυσιάσουσιν" RSV NRSV REB "(offerings) are brought" GNT "(offerings) are burnt" \| NJPS "built up high"

Xuan Huong Pham

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 49:15; Isaiah 46:7; Isaiah 53:4; Isaiah 53:11; Lamentations 5:7; Isaiah 46:4; Ecclesiastes 12:5; Psalms 144:14; Ezra 6:3

to make a turn \= action by which humans leave the road they are travelling on to engage in other activities, often with the purpose to continue on they way later

## סוּר (id: 005040000000000)

סוּר
====

סוּר (H5494 · H5495)

adj · סור

Unfaithful

turning away \= action by which humans stop engaging in a certain type of behavior, and start to be involved in other activities, ◄ described as people leaving the road they are travelling on

[JER 17:13](https://ref.ly/Jer17:13)

Bad

degenerate, corrupt literally: turning away; hence: \= process by which a plant has loses certain qualities that used to make it a special variety

[JER 2:21](https://ref.ly/Jer2:21)

Unwilling

put away, rejected literally: turned away; hence: \= state in which other people are no longer willing to associate someone

[ISA 49:21](https://ref.ly/Isa49:21)

name

Names of Constructions

**Collocation:** שַׁעַר סוּר

Sur Gate \= one of the gates of the temple in Jerusalem

[2KI 11:6](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:6)

1 JER 17:13 MT\-K יסורי \| MT\-Q סוּרַי

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Jeremiah 17:13; Jeremiah 2:21; Isaiah 49:21; 2 Kings 11:6

## סחר (id: 005049000000000)

## סֹךְ (id: 005068000000000)

סֹךְ
====

סֹךְ (H5520)

noun m · סכך

Tents

booth, hut, lair \= a shelter, ◄ made of fragile materials such as leaves and branches, ► for the purpose of protection from rain and sun for both humans and animals; used by people who needed a temporary shelter, such as nomads, soldiers, and farm workers in the field; ≈ by extension, figuratively God's protection over his people, God's shelter for himself; also a metaphor for Jerusalem, the dwelling of God's people; also by extension, a place where ferocious animals can hide in order to attack someone

## סכך (id: 005074000000000)

סכך
===

סכך (H5526a · H5526b · H5526c · H5526e · H5526f) — שׂכך

verb · מוּסָךְ · מָסָךְ · מְסֻכָה · סָךְ · סֹךְ · סֻכָּה · סֹכֵךְ

Cover

to cover \= state in which a piece of cloth is spread out over a surface

[ISA 25:7](https://ref.ly/Isa25:7)

Cover

to cover oneself \= action by which deities cover themselves with an object

[LAM 3:44](https://ref.ly/Lam3:44)

Cover

to cover, to screen off, to shelter \= causative action by which a certain area is covered from above or from the side, ► so as to make it invisible or inaccesible, or to provide shelter for it

[EXO 25:20](https://ref.ly/Exod25:20) · [EXO 33:22](https://ref.ly/Exod33:22) · [EXO 37:9](https://ref.ly/Exod37:9) · [EXO 40:3](https://ref.ly/Exod40:3) · [EXO 40:21](https://ref.ly/Exod40:21) · [1KI 8:7](https://ref.ly/1Kgs8:7) · [1CH 28:18](https://ref.ly/1Chr28:18) · [JOB 40:22](https://ref.ly/Job40:22) · [PSA 91:4](https://ref.ly/Ps91:4) · [PSA 140:8](https://ref.ly/Ps140:8) · [EZK 28:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:14) · [EZK 28:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek28:16)

Close

to shut in literally: to cover; hence: \= action by which deities close an opening with an object to prevent a substance from coming out

[JOB 38:8](https://ref.ly/Job38:8)

Engage

to cover onself (with an activity), to engage (in an activity) literally: to cover oneself; hence: \= action by which deities engage themselves in a certain activity

[LAM 3:43](https://ref.ly/Lam3:43)

Excrete

**Collocation:** סכך רַגְלַיִם

to cover (one's) feet \> to relieve oneself literally: to cover (one's) feet; hence: \= action by which humans squat down in order to relieve themselves, as a result of which their robe covers their feet

[JDG 3:24](https://ref.ly/Judg3:24) · [1SA 24:4](https://ref.ly/1Sam24:4)

Safe

to hedge in, to hedge about, to shelter, to defend literally: to cover; hence: \= causative action by which a deity provides protection to humans, ◄ as if by covering them on all sides

[JOB 3:23](https://ref.ly/Job3:23) · [PSA 5:12](https://ref.ly/Ps5:12)

verb

Weave

to weave \= causative action by which humans produce fabric by weaving; ≈ exclusively used in a figurative way for God causing an unborn child to grow in its mother's womb

[JOB 10:11](https://ref.ly/Job10:11) · [PSA 139:13](https://ref.ly/Ps139:13)

Reinier de Blois

## סֹכֵךְ (id: 005075000000000)

סֹכֵךְ
======

סֹכֵךְ (H5526d)

noun m · סכך

Weapons

protective shield, mantelet literally: covering; hence: \= a large protective shield used for covering the soldiers who operated a battering ram, who were exposed to attack from above by the defenders of the city; sometimes the mantelet was part of the mechanism that carried the battering ram; sometimes it was formed by other soldiers who overlapped individual shields above their heads

[NAM 2:6](https://ref.ly/Nah2:6)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Nahum 2:6

Grieve

to mourn \= action by which human perform the mourning ritual for someone who has died, or for another tragic event; this may include wailing, tearing one's clothes, putting on sackcloth, covering oneself with dust or ashes, fasting or eating specific food, cutting oneself, shaving one's head, covering part of one's face, etc.; this usually takes place during a specific period of time and ends after the burial has taken place, but it may also be repeated in later days to commemorate a tragic event

סתר (H5641 · A5642a · A5642b)

verb · מִסְתֹּור · מִסְתָּר · מַסְתֵּר · סֵתֶר · סִתְרָה · סְתוּר

Hide

to be hidden \= state in which people or objects are in a location where they cannot be readily seen or where danger cannot reach them

[GEN 4:14](https://ref.ly/Gen4:14) · [GEN 31:49](https://ref.ly/Gen31:49) · [JOB 28:21](https://ref.ly/Job28:21) · [ZEP 2:3](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:3)

Hide

to hide oneself \= action by which humans go to a location where they will not be readily seen or where danger cannot reach them

[DEU 7:20](https://ref.ly/Deut7:20) · [1SA 20:5](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:5) · [1SA 20:19](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:19) · [1SA 20:24](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:24) · [1SA 23:19](https://ref.ly/1Sam23:19) · [1SA 26:1](https://ref.ly/1Sam26:1) · [1KI 17:3](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:3) · [JOB 13:20](https://ref.ly/Job13:20) · [JOB 34:22](https://ref.ly/Job34:22) · [PSA 54:2](https://ref.ly/Ps54:2) · [PSA 55:13](https://ref.ly/Ps55:13) · [PSA 89:47](https://ref.ly/Ps89:47) · [PRO 22:3](https://ref.ly/Prov22:3) · [PRO 27:12](https://ref.ly/Prov27:12) · [PRO 28:28](https://ref.ly/Prov28:28) · [ISA 28:15](https://ref.ly/Isa28:15) · [ISA 45:15](https://ref.ly/Isa45:15) · [JER 23:24](https://ref.ly/Jer23:24) · [JER 36:19](https://ref.ly/Jer36:19) · [AMO 9:3](https://ref.ly/Amos9:3)

Hide

to hide, to conceal \= causative action by which humans or deities cause (other) humans to go to a location where they will not be readily seen or where danger cannot reach them

[2KI 11:2](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:2) · [2CH 22:11](https://ref.ly/2Chr22:11) · [JOB 3:10](https://ref.ly/Job3:10) · [JOB 14:13](https://ref.ly/Job14:13) · [PSA 17:8](https://ref.ly/Ps17:8) · [PSA 27:5](https://ref.ly/Ps27:5) · [PSA 31:21](https://ref.ly/Ps31:21) · [PSA 64:3](https://ref.ly/Ps64:3) · [ISA 16:3](https://ref.ly/Isa16:3) · [ISA 49:2](https://ref.ly/Isa49:2) · [JER 36:26](https://ref.ly/Jer36:26)

Non\-See

**Collocation:** סתר פָּנֶה

to hide (one's) face literally: to hide (one's) face; hence: \= causative action by which humans cover their face in order to be unable to see or be seen

[EXO 3:6](https://ref.ly/Exod3:6) · [ISA 50:6](https://ref.ly/Isa50:6)

Non\-Feel

to be hidden \> to feel not literally: to be hidden; hence: \= state by which the effect of something is not perceived physically

[PSA 19:7](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7)

Non\-Know

to be hidden, to be unknown, hidden, secret \= state in which certain information is not generally known, ◄ as if it were physically hidden

[NUM 5:13](https://ref.ly/Num5:13) · [DEU 29:28](https://ref.ly/Deut29:28) · [JOB 3:23](https://ref.ly/Job3:23) · [PSA 19:13](https://ref.ly/Ps19:13) · [PSA 38:10](https://ref.ly/Ps38:10) · [ISA 29:14](https://ref.ly/Isa29:14) · [ISA 40:27](https://ref.ly/Isa40:27) · [ISA 65:16](https://ref.ly/Isa65:16) · [JER 16:17](https://ref.ly/Jer16:17) · [DAN 2:22](https://ref.ly/Dan2:22) · [HOS 13:14](https://ref.ly/Hos13:14)

Non\-Know

to hide, to keep from knowing, to conceal \= causative action by which humans or deities cause others not to be aware of certain information, ◄ as if by physically hiding it

[1SA 20:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam20:2) · [PSA 119:19](https://ref.ly/Ps119:19) · [PRO 25:2](https://ref.ly/Prov25:2) · [PRO 27:5](https://ref.ly/Prov27:5) · [ISA 29:15](https://ref.ly/Isa29:15)

Unwilling

**Collocation:** סתר פָּנֶה

to hide (one's) face, to reject literally: to hide (one's) face (from someone); hence: \= action by which a deity does not engage with people, and does not intervene neither in their favor nor to punish, ◄ as if he were enable to see them

[DEU 31:17](https://ref.ly/Deut31:17) · [DEU 31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:18) · [DEU 31:18](https://ref.ly/Deut31:18) · [DEU 32:20](https://ref.ly/Deut32:20) · [JOB 13:24](https://ref.ly/Job13:24) · [JOB 34:29](https://ref.ly/Job34:29) · [PSA 10:11](https://ref.ly/Ps10:11) · [PSA 13:2](https://ref.ly/Ps13:2) · [PSA 22:25](https://ref.ly/Ps22:25) · [PSA 27:9](https://ref.ly/Ps27:9) · [PSA 30:8](https://ref.ly/Ps30:8) · [PSA 44:25](https://ref.ly/Ps44:25) · [PSA 51:11](https://ref.ly/Ps51:11) · [PSA 69:18](https://ref.ly/Ps69:18) · [PSA 88:15](https://ref.ly/Ps88:15) · [PSA 102:3](https://ref.ly/Ps102:3) · [PSA 104:29](https://ref.ly/Ps104:29) · [PSA 143:7](https://ref.ly/Ps143:7) · [ISA 8:17](https://ref.ly/Isa8:17) · [ISA 54:8](https://ref.ly/Isa54:8) · [ISA 57:17](https://ref.ly/Isa57:17) · [ISA 59:2](https://ref.ly/Isa59:2) · [ISA 64:6](https://ref.ly/Isa64:6) · [JER 33:5](https://ref.ly/Jer33:5) · [EZK 39:23](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:23) · [EZK 39:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:24) · [EZK 39:29](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:29) · [MIC 3:4](https://ref.ly/Mic3:4)

verb

Non\-Exist

to destroy \= causative action by which one puts an end to the existence of something by damaging it

[EZR 5:12](https://ref.ly/Ezra5:12)

Steve Berneking

## סֵתֶר (id: 005190000000000)

סֵתֶר
=====

סֵתֶר (H5643a)

noun m · סתר

Hide

cover, shelter, disguise \= state in which people, animals, or objects are in a location where they cannot be readily seen or where danger cannot reach them

[1SA 25:20](https://ref.ly/1Sam25:20) · [JOB 22:14](https://ref.ly/Job22:14) · [JOB 24:15](https://ref.ly/Job24:15) · [JOB 40:21](https://ref.ly/Job40:21) · [PSA 18:12](https://ref.ly/Ps18:12) · [PSA 27:5](https://ref.ly/Ps27:5) · [PSA 31:21](https://ref.ly/Ps31:21) · [PSA 61:5](https://ref.ly/Ps61:5) · [PSA 81:8](https://ref.ly/Ps81:8) · [PSA 91:1](https://ref.ly/Ps91:1) · [PSA 139:15](https://ref.ly/Ps139:15) · [SNG 2:14](https://ref.ly/Song2:14) · [ISA 16:4](https://ref.ly/Isa16:4) · [ISA 28:17](https://ref.ly/Isa28:17) · [ISA 32:2](https://ref.ly/Isa32:2)

Non\-Know

secret, secrecy \= state in which knowledge, an object, or an action is kept hidden or unknown from others

[DEU 13:7](https://ref.ly/Deut13:7) · [DEU 27:15](https://ref.ly/Deut27:15) · [DEU 27:24](https://ref.ly/Deut27:24) · [DEU 28:57](https://ref.ly/Deut28:57) · [JDG 3:19](https://ref.ly/Judg3:19) · [1SA 19:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam19:2) · [2SA 12:12](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:12) · [JOB 13:10](https://ref.ly/Job13:10) · [JOB 31:27](https://ref.ly/Job31:27) · [PSA 101:5](https://ref.ly/Ps101:5) · [PRO 9:17](https://ref.ly/Prov9:17) · [PRO 21:14](https://ref.ly/Prov21:14) · [PRO 25:23](https://ref.ly/Prov25:23) · [ISA 45:19](https://ref.ly/Isa45:19) · [ISA 48:16](https://ref.ly/Isa48:16) · [JER 37:17](https://ref.ly/Jer37:17) · [JER 38:16](https://ref.ly/Jer38:16) · [JER 40:15](https://ref.ly/Jer40:15)

Titles

Shelter literally: (one's) shelter; hence: \= a title for God as the one who provides a hiding place for his people

[PSA 32:7](https://ref.ly/Ps32:7) · [PSA 119:114](https://ref.ly/Ps119:114)

Steve Berneking

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Samuel 25:20; Job 22:14; Job 24:15; Job 40:21; Psalms 18:12; Psalms 27:5; Psalms 31:21; Psalms 61:5; Psalms 81:8; Psalms 91:1; Psalms 139:15; Song of Songs 2:14; Isaiah 16:4; Isaiah 28:17; Isaiah 32:2; Deuteronomy 13:7; Deuteronomy 27:15; Deuteronomy 27:24; Deuteronomy 28:57; Judges 3:19; 1 Samuel 19:2; 2 Samuel 12:12; Job 13:10; Job 31:27; Psalms 101:5; Proverbs 9:17; Proverbs 21:14; Proverbs 25:23; Isaiah 45:19; Isaiah 48:16; Jeremiah 37:17; Jeremiah 38:16; Jeremiah 40:15; Psalms 32:7; Psalms 119:114

סִתְרָה (H5643b)

shelter literally: shelter; \= people who provide security to other people
